***бриз.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бриз</a> (23118)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from some Western European language, most likely from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">breeze</i>. Further etymology unknown.
</p><p>Initially attested in 1718 in form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бри́зами</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brízami</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the context of names of different kinds of winds in Portugal. This instrumental plural form is likely not from modern spelling <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бриз</a></i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">briz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, but from an exact rendering of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">brisa</i>, which would be <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*<a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бри́за</a></i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*briza</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (both have identical case forms in plural).
</p><p>Judging by the lack of further attestations in the 18th century, the term didn't settle in the language until 19th century (and from a different source).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бриз</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">briz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бри́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бри́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бриз.html>бри́зов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sea breeze</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бритва.html>бри́тва</a> (6291)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*britva</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*briti</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-tva</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брить.html>брить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">britʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***брить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:брить.html>брить</a> (15844)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*brìti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брить.html>брить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">britʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">бръвь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brŭvĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bry</i>.
</p>

***бродить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бродить.html>броди́ть</a> (2275)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">бродити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">broditi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*brodìti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰrodʰ-eye-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰredʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бродить.html>броди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">brodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to wander, to roam, to ramble
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бродить.html>броди́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́роду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>но́чью</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne <b>brodí</b> po górodu nóčʹju</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Do not wander through the city at night.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to stroll
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бродить.html>брожу́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́роду</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>brožú</b> po górodu.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I’m strolling about the city.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одному́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бродить.html>броди́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скучно.html>ску́чно</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Odnomú <b>brodítʹ</b> skúšno/skúčno.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It is boring to stroll alone.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:завтра.html>за́втра</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пойду́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бродить.html>броди́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лесу</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>ле́су</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>závtra</b> pojdú <b>brodítʹ</b> pó lesu/po lésu.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Tomorrow I will go for a stroll through the forest.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to ferment</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бродить.html>Броди́ть</a></b> is a Russian abstract verb. Its counterpart, <a href = vnd.unilang:брести.html>брести́</a>, is a concrete verb.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бродить.html>броди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брожение.html>броже́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">brožénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брожение.html>броже́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брожение.html>броже́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брожение.html>броже́ний</a></b>)

***бронебойный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бронебойный.html>бронебо́йный</a> (25127)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1889 [see citations]. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:броня.html>броня́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bronjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бой</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">panzerbrechend</i> [Arapova].

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:броненосец.html>бронено́сец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bronenósec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:броненосец.html>бронено́сца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:броненосец.html>бронено́сцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:броненосец.html>бронено́сцев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> battleship (pre-dreadnought type), ironclad</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бронепоезд.html>бронепо́езд</a> (21186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:броня.html>броня́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bronjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>по́езд</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pójezd</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Panzerzug</i>, according to Arapova.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бронзовый.html>бро́нзовый</a> (4709)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бронза.html>бро́нза</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brónza</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бронзовый.html>бро́нзовый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">brónzovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bronze
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бронзовый.html>бро́нзовый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:век.html>век</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>brónzovyj</b> vek</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Bronze</b> Age</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бронза.html>бро́нза</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">brónza</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бронированный.html>брониро́ванный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">broniróvannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бронирова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bronirovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бронирова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bronirovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бронированный.html>брониро́ванный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">broniróvannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>armored <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">clad or equipped with armor</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бронированный.html>брониро́ванный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:автомобиль.html>автомоби́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>broniróvannyj</b> avtomobílʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">armored car</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>bulletproof, armor <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">describing a material</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бронированный.html>брониро́ванное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стекло́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>broniróvannoje</b> stekló</i> ― <span class="e-translation">bulletproof glass</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бронированный.html>брониро́ванная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:плита.html>плита́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>broniróvannaja</b> plitá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">armor plate</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***броня.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:броня.html>броня</a> (6237)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">бръня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brŭnja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*brъňa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌱𐍂𐌿𐌽𐌾𐍉</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brunjō</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*brunjǭ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:броня.html>броня́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bronjá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:броня.html>брони́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:броня.html>брони́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:броня.html>броне́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> armor, armour, armoring, shell</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Developed from the sense of “armor” during the Soviet period. Sense development was from “armor” → “securing” → “reservation”.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:броня.html>бро́ня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">brónja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:броня.html>бро́ни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:броня.html>бро́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:броня.html>бро́нь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>reservation, booking</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">резерви́рование</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rezervírovanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:броня.html>бро́нь</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bronʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***бросать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бросать.html>броса́ть</a> (1444)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*brъsati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бросать.html>броса́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">brosátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бросить.html>бро́сить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw, to drop
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>начал</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бросать.html>броса́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мяч.html>мяч</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja načal <b>brosátʹ</b> mjač.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I started to throw the ball.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to send urgently</li>
<li>to abandon, to forsake</li>
<li>to give up, to quit, to leave off</li>
<li>to jilt</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бросать.html>броса́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brosátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бросаться.html>броса́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">brosátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:броситься.html>бро́ситься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fling <i>(oneself)</i>, to dash, to rush</li>
